You are at the age of service and at the time of national revival. The country is complete. We hope for your virtue and majesty in the future. We look forward to your songs in the years to come. We send our congratulations and hope you will accept them." Chen Yue, the director of the China Mass Art Construction Association, kowtows.

Dagong Vocational School: In addition to hanging lanterns and decorations on the 31st, the teachers and students of Dagong Vocational School on Longhua Road also purchased a large number of fireworks starting at 7:00 PM that evening to hold a celebration for Chiang Kai-shek's birthday and a party. They lectured on Chiang Kai-shek's revolutionary history, thought, and achievements. After the lectures, there were more than 50 entertainment programs, which were very popular. The school's congratulatory telegram is recorded below: "To Chairman Chiang: We respectfully celebrate your birthday and wish you good health. All the staff and students of Shanghai Dagong Vocational School kowtow."

The grand celebration of the Civic Education Center (International News Agency Photo)

National Boy Scout Inspection Results Announced

First Place: Zhejiang; Second Place: Nanjing; Third Place: Jiangsu

(Special dispatch from Nanjing) The China Boy Scout General Association held its fifth judging committee meeting on the morning of the 30th. The attendees were Zhu Jiahua, Gu Shusen, Gui Yongqing, Song Xishang, Yuan Zongze, and others. The chairman was Zhu Jiahua. They reviewed the performance results and rankings of the provinces, as well as the allocation of prizes. It was found that Nanjing was the best in the inspection, followed by Zhejiang. Zhejiang was the best in camping, followed by Jiangsu. Zhejiang was the best in curriculum, followed by Nanjing. Nanjing was the best in labor service, followed by Zhejiang. The overall rankings are as follows: First Place: Zhejiang; Second Place: Nanjing; Third Place: Jiangsu; Fourth Place: Hubei; Fifth Place: Nanning; Sixth Place: Hankou; Seventh Place: Anhui; Eighth Place: Hunan; Ninth Place: Shanghai; Tenth Place: Chahar; Eleventh Place: Gansu; Twelfth Place: Shaanxi; Thirteenth Place: Henan; Fourteenth Place: Jiangxi; Fifteenth Place: Guangzhou; Sixteenth Place: Beiping; Seventeenth Place: Fujian; Eighteenth Place: Shanxi; Nineteenth Place: Yunnan; Twentieth Place: Tianjin. Provinces such as Guizhou, Shandong, Suiyuan, Guangdong, Qingdao, and Hebei were ranked lower because they did not participate in all the events.

Overview of Departments Established by National Independent Colleges

The following is a summary of the recent departments established by national, provincial, and private independent colleges across the country, based on the recent survey statistics of the Ministry of Education:

(1) Among the five national colleges, the Shanghai College of Commerce's commerce department is divided into four departments: Accounting, Business Administration, Banking, and International Trade. The Shanghai Medical College's medical department is not divided. The Sino-French National Institute of Technology's engineering department is divided into four departments: Civil Engineering, Railway, Mechanical Engineering, and Electrical Engineering. The Beiyang Institute of Technology's engineering department is divided into four departments: Civil Engineering, Metallurgy, Mechanical Engineering, and Electrical Engineering (with an affiliated Institute of Engineering Technology, Department of Mining and Metallurgy). The Guangdong College of Law is divided into two departments: Law and Political Science.

(2) Among the nine provincial colleges, the Jiangsu College of Education's education department is divided into two departments: Public Education and Agricultural Education (with affiliated Agricultural Education and Film and Broadcasting Education specialized courses). The Hubei College of Education's education department is divided into two departments: Agricultural Education and Rural Education (with affiliated Rural Normal and Agricultural Education specialized courses). The Hebei Institute of Technology's engineering department is divided into three departments: Mechanical and Electrical Engineering, Chemical Manufacturing, and Municipal Water Conservancy Engineering. The Hebei Women's Normal College's liberal arts department is divided into seven departments: Chinese, English, History and Geography, Education, Home Economics, Physical Education, and Music specialized courses (the English and Education departments have stopped enrolling students). The Hebei College of Law and Commerce's law department is divided into two departments: Law and Political Economy. The commerce department has one department: Commerce (the Political Economy departments stopped enrolling students in 1935 and were discontinued). The Hebei College of Agriculture's agriculture department is divided into three departments: Forestry, Agriculture, and Horticulture. The Hebei Medical College's medical department is not divided. The Gansu College's liberal arts department is divided into two departments: Literature and History, and Chinese Literature. The law department has one department: Law. The Xinjiang College's law department is divided into three departments: Law, Political Science, and Economics (with an affiliated Taxation specialized course).

(3) Among the twenty-three private colleges, in addition to the seven colleges that have not divided departments, including the Peking Union Medical College, the Aurora University, the Guangdong Guanghua Medical College, the Xiangya Medical College, the Shanghai Women's Medical College, the Tongde Medical College, and the Southeast Medical College, the Ginling College for Women's Arts and Sciences' science department is divided into three departments: Mathematics and Physics, Chemistry, and Biology. The liberal arts department is divided into nine departments: Chinese, English, History, Sociology, Philosophy, Political Science, Economics, Physical Education, and Music (ordered to submit a plan for merging departments for review). The Shanghai Law College's law department is divided into Law, Politics and Economics, and Commerce specialized courses). The Shanghai College of Law and Politics' law department is divided into three departments: Political Science, Economics, and Law. The Chih Tze College's liberal arts department is divided into Chinese and English. The law department is divided into Law, Politics and Economics, and Business (the English department has been suspended since 1935). The Zhengfeng College of Arts' liberal arts department is divided into Chinese Literature and Chinese specialized courses. The China College's liberal arts department has Literature, the law department has Law, and the commerce department has Commerce (ordered to continue until the existing students graduate). The China College's science department is divided into Chemistry and Biology, the liberal arts department is divided into Chinese Studies, English Philosophy Education, and the law department is divided into Law, Politics, and Economics (the English department stopped enrolling new students and was discontinued). The Chaoyang College's law department is divided into Law, Political Science, Economics, and Border Politics (the Border Politics department stopped enrolling students in 1936). The Beiping Republic College's liberal arts department is divided into Chinese Education, and Physical Education specialized courses. The law department is divided into Law, Political Science, and Economics. The Tianjin Institute of Technology and Commerce's engineering department is divided into Mechanical and Civil Engineering. The commerce department is divided into General Commerce, Finance, and Banking. The Nantong College's agriculture department is divided into Agronomy, Chemistry, and Agriculture. The medical department is not divided (with an affiliated Textile department). The Soochow University's science department is divided into Chemistry and Civil Engineering. The liberal arts department is divided into Chinese, English, Economics, Political Science, and Education. The Fukien Christian University's science department is divided into Mathematics, Chemistry, Biology, Agriculture, and Agricultural Economics. The liberal arts department is divided into Chinese, Foreign Languages, Education, Political Economy, History, and Society (the Political Economy, History, and Society departments stopped enrolling students in 1936). The Hwa Nan College for Women's Arts and Sciences' science department is divided into Chemistry and Biology. The liberal arts department is divided into English and Education. The Fukien College's law department is divided into Law, Political Science, and Economics. The agricultural department is divided into Agronomy (the law department has been ordered to close; the Law department is temporarily allowed to enroll students this year). The Jiaozuo Institute of Technology's engineering department is divided into Civil Engineering, Mining, and Metallurgy.

Chiang Kai-shek's Fiftieth Birthday Celebrated by All Sectors Yesterday; Grand Celebrations by Government, Business, and Citizens in this City

Yesterday was Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. The entire nation celebrated enthusiastically. Besides the aircraft dedication ceremony held in Nanjing at 9:00 AM for Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, the Shanghai Municipal Government and its affiliated agencies held a luncheon celebration. Groups such as the Public Education Center and the Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association held separate celebrations. Leaders from all walks of life held a simple but enthusiastic celebration ceremony at 2:00 PM in the Huang Family Garden in Caohejing, as well as a grand entertainment and amusement fair. Details are reported as follows:

City-wide Flag Display, Enthusiastic Celebration

All stores, companies, factories, and residences throughout the city uniformly displayed flags and decorations to mark the occasion. Qing Tian Bai Ri (Blue Sky with a White Sun) national flags were hung high along all the roads, fluttering in the wind, presenting a spectacular sight. In addition to hanging flags and decorations, stores also set up window displays featuring portraits of Generalissimo Chiang and Party-State flags. Nanjing Road was the most lively area, with the four major companies (Wing On, Sincere, Sun Sun, and The Sun) using electric lights to create various congratulatory messages, which were hung at their entrances. The Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association also used electric lights on the eighteenth floor of the Wing On Company's new building to form the large characters "Respectfully Wishing Generalissimo Chiang a Happy Birthday," which were brightly lit at night, making them even more beautiful. The municipal military police authorities and the police departments of the two concessions increased patrols due to the surge in pedestrian traffic, and intensified security for the day.

Nanjing Road Business Community's One-Day Donation

The Nanjing Road business community in this city, because the road is located in the bustling center, its expressions are sufficient to influence popular sentiment and convey [messages] to friendly countries. Therefore, on the occasion of Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday yesterday, they specially requested the Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association's Citizen District Branch to lead all the stores on the road in making efforts to decorate in a celebratory manner. The Association made 1,200 colored lanterns and distributed them to the stores to hang up, as well as 2,000 slogans such as "Unanimously Supporting the Hard-Working and Meritorious Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek" and "Respectfully Wishing the Unique Revolutionary Leader Generalissimo Chiang a Happy Fiftieth Birthday," which were posted on the store doors. They also lit a large electric light display of the characters "Respectfully Wishing Generalissimo Chiang a Happy Birthday" in the Wing On New Building, which was several yards in diameter. The whole road was brightly lit at night, with tourists filling the streets, creating an unprecedented scene. The major companies and several Western clothing stores also decorated their entrances and window displays with innovative congratulatory lanterns and decorations, which were particularly eye-catching. As for the one-day campaign of all stores on the road on October 30th, donating 10% of their business revenue, the Wing On Company has reported a total of 2,160 yuan, Sincere reported 1,532 yuan, and Sun Sun Company will base its donation on yesterday's business. Other stores donated amounts ranging from 300-400 yuan to 20-30 yuan. Once all the funds have been collected, the Association will publish an advertisement in the newspaper for creditability, and remit the funds to the Aircraft Purchase for Birthday Celebration Committee, in order to strengthen air defense.

Radio Broadcasts and Projection of Portraits

The city's radio stations, in celebration of Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, broadcasted various special programs. Yesterday afternoon at 1:30 PM, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, gave a broadcast speech, discussing the significance of celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday. In addition, various groups including the National Conservatory of Music, the Public Education Center's Peking Opera troupe, the Public Safety Bureau's military band, and the Shanghai Amusement Association's Shanghai opera, Suzhou ballad, comedy, drama, Run Yu Society, Yong Yu Society, improved national opera, Huaiyang storytelling, and story broadcast teams, all mobilized to broadcast various high-quality programs in celebration. At the same time, all the city's cinemas projected portraits of Generalissimo Chiang before the film screenings, and the audience stood up to pay their respects.

Vice President Kong Sends Congratulatory Telegram

Administrative Vice-President and Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, being ill in Shanghai, was unable to personally congratulate Generalissimo Chiang on his birthday, so he sent a special congratulatory telegram. The telegram read: "To Generalissimo Chiang in Luoyang, On this day, as we respectfully celebrate your birthday, people near and far rejoice, and the nine provinces praise you. You, sir, with the hand of turning heaven and earth, have achieved the merit of rescuing the endangered and pacifying the chaos. Leading the multitudes, you have laid the foundation of China. Your great achievements shine brightly throughout the world. Praising virtue and extolling merit, the people cherish and celebrate together. And you, sir, with your great virtue and humility, decline because of the difficult times. The whole country admires and respects you beyond words. I, who have long known you deeply and have shared weal and woe as a brother, dare not disturb your ears with cumbersome formalities. However, seeing the nationwide acclamation and the purchasing of aircraft as a birthday gift, I can see the people's love and support, and thus foresee the revival of the nation. I wish you, not for your own sake, but truly for the strength of the country. Lying ill in Shanghai, unable to attend. I respectfully offer these simple words to extend my congratulations. Your brother Kong Xiangxi, respectfully at Shanghai. [Seal]"

Municipal Government Colleagues Gather for Lunch Celebration

The Shanghai Municipal Government and its affiliated bureaus of Social Affairs, Public Safety, Public Utilities, Finance, Land, Public Works, and Health, held a luncheon for colleagues at 12:30 PM yesterday in the municipal government auditorium in the city center, to celebrate Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. All staff members above the section staff level participated, with over 500 people attending, including Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Secretaries Sun Pu, Geng Jiaji, Zhang Tingrong, Hong Da, Zhang Yuanruo, Chen Kecheng, Tang Shixuan, Commissioner Wang Changchun, and Bureau Directors Pan Gongzhan, Cai Jinjun, Li Tingan, Xu Peihuang, Xu Fu, and Shen Yi. Because Mayor Wu Tiecheng represented Shanghai in going to Nanjing to present the aircraft, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun led the birthday celebration on his behalf. The ceremony was simple but solemn. The entire group stood and sang the Party song, and chanted "Long live Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek." They dispersed at around 2:00 PM, having enjoyed the occasion.

City-wide Party Members' Birthday Celebration Luncheon

In addition to erecting a colorful archway at the entrance and sending a telegram congratulating Generalissimo Chiang, the city's Party Headquarters, due to the enthusiasm and excitement of all Party members in celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, specially decided to hold a joyful gathering for all Party members yesterday at 6:30 PM at the Atlantic Western Restaurant on Fourth Road, to celebrate Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday. Over 500 people attended, including staff members from the City Party Headquarters and district Party Headquarters, and representatives from various district branches. The event was presided over by Standing Committee member Pan Gongzhan. The ceremony was as follows: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party-State flag and the portrait of the Founding Father; (4) Respectfully read the Founding Father's will; (5) Chairman's report; (6) Pay birthday greetings to the portrait of Generalissimo Chiang; (7) Cheer slogans; (8) Start the luncheon; (9) Take a photo; (10) Adjourn. During the luncheon, the Chairman reported on Generalissimo Chiang's history of striving for revolution and laying the foundation for the country, as well as the significance of the celebration, and said that Generalissimo Chiang is our comrades' only leader, and that under his leadership, our efforts and progress will give great hope to the nation's future, and that today's enthusiastic birthday celebration is a sincere expression of support for the leader, and so on. Tao Baichuan then delivered a speech. The length of his words is omitted. They cheered slogans and adjourned around 9:00 PM.

Public Education Center Celebration Rally

The Municipal Public Education Center held a celebration rally yesterday for Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. Approximately 1,000 people attended, including all staff members of the center, students from the center's affiliated schools, and members of the martial arts, harmonica, singing, and Peking Opera teams. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, was invited to speak about Generalissimo Chiang's revolutionary achievements. The meeting opened at 9:00 AM. In addition to following the usual meeting procedures, the attendees also paid birthday greetings to Generalissimo Chiang with the highest respect, and sang the commemorative song for Generalissimo Chiang's birthday. After the song, Xu Zexiang, the director of the center, reported on the purpose of the meeting in very brief words, saying, "The center has received orders and dare not be extravagant, so everything is very simple." He also said that the most important thing for us to recognize at this commemorative celebration is the greatness of Generalissimo Chiang's personality and career, which is deeply moving. Director Pan will then talk about Generalissimo Chiang's revolutionary achievements. The main points can be divided into two: one is Generalissimo Chiang's twenty-five years of filial piety, and the other is his twenty-five years of serving the country. He also said that at this celebration, we should have absolute faith in and support for Generalissimo Chiang, so that we can save the country from extinction, revive the nation, and achieve our goals. Finally, he used Generalissimo Chiang's deeds of loyalty and filial piety to encourage the people. The speech lasted for over an hour, and the audience was quite moved. Finally, two students from the center's schools, Xu Liying and Xu Lili, gave speeches. One spoke about the significance of celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, and the other spoke about why we should celebrate Generalissimo Chiang. Both speeches were brief and to the point. Around 11:00 AM, the photo was taken and the ceremony was completed. At that time, the entire center, both inside and out, was decorated with high-hanging arches and colorful lanterns, with tens of thousands of people gathered, and the atmosphere was enthusiastic. Its grandeur was unprecedented.

Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association Celebration Rally

The Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai held a celebration rally yesterday for Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. A colorful electric light archway made of pine and cypress was erected at the gate, with the words "Celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's Fiftieth Birthday" prominently displayed. The auditorium was set up in the hall. From morning to noon, over 10,000 people attended the celebration, including association members Yu Qiaqing, Xu Shengchan, Fang Jiaobo, Yue Zhenbao, Mao Heyuan, Zhu Meixian, Huang Yanfang, Yu Zuoting, Liu Hongsheng, Liu Pinsan, Chen Zhonggao, Mu Zixiang, Ye Xianggao, Chen Yiting, Zhang Jiguang, Chen Liangyu, Shi Zhikun, Wu Yaqin, Hu Xiyuan, Ying Sunling, and fellow townsmen Zhou Wuming, Sheng Pihua, Mao Songting, Xu Wenxia, Zhang Baiming. Yu Qiaqing was publicly elected as chairman, Dong Xinqin as master of ceremonies, and Zhao Kuiyi as recorder. All stood at attention and paid their respects to the Party-State flag and the portrait of Generalissimo Chiang. Then the association's elementary school students sang the Party song. The chairman of the board delivered an opening speech, saying, "Today is the fiftieth birthday of our national leader, the hard-working and meritorious Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek. Generalissimo Chiang has devoted himself to the National Revolution without shirking hardships. Since the Northern Expedition in 1926, he has overcome numerous hardships to seek the revival of our nation and to fight for national rights for our country. Through many struggles, he has finally achieved the goal of national unification. Now, in this year of abundant harvests, on the day of Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday, in addition to donating funds to purchase an aircraft, and publicly appointing Mr. Fu Xiao'an to go to Beijing to participate in the presentation ceremony, we specially invite fellow townsmen to remotely offer our congratulations and express our sincere love and support." He then shouted "Long live Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek" and "Long live the Republic of China" three times. Zhu Meixian then gave a speech, encouraging his fellow townsmen to love and support the leader of the Republic of China, and to obey the leader's directives. The leader instructs us to promote: (1) the New Life Movement, (2) national military education, and (3) national economic construction, in order to achieve national strength and prosperity. He cited the emerging facts of Germany and Italy as metaphors, and his words were extremely vigilant. Next, the commemorative song was sung. From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM, famous Peking Opera performers were invited to put on a show to add to the fun. The program included: (1) a group performance of "Boundless Longevity", (2) Mr. Li Boshan's "Majesty Shakes the Grass Bridge," (3) Mr. Guan Hongbin's "Paradise State," (4) Miss Ji's "Candlelight Plot," (5) Zhao Junshuai's "Golden Lock Record," and (6) Mr. Mao Yanweng's "Aspiring to Join the Army."

Leaders from All Walks of Life's Joyful Gathering

Yesterday was Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. Over 1,000 leaders from all walks of life in this city, including Yu Qiaqing, held a grand birthday celebration and joyful gathering at Huang's Garden in Caohejing yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Over 1,000 people attended, including Yu Qiaqing, Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Yang Hu, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Qun, Lu Jingshi, Huang Renzhi, Guo Bingwen, Zhu Xuefan, Yuan Ludeng, Xu Jilou, Shao Xubai, Fang Jiaobo, Xi Guansheng, Zhu Wenqi, Qin Runqing, Zhang Kechang, Guo Shun, Chu Huiseng, Mao Zijian, Zhou Xuexiang, Li Mengnan, Wang Yiting, Zhao Xien, Qu Wenliu, Hu Xiyuan, Pan Gongzhan, Cai Zengji, He Dekui, Wu Yuncho, Wu Yunzhai, Zhou Zuomin, Yan Fuqing, and Shen Junru. At 2:30 PM, they gathered in the Fourth Teaching Hall, led by the presidium of Yu Qiaqing, Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Qian Xinzhi, Yang Hu, and Huang Renzhi, to perform the birthday celebration ceremony. The ceremony was simple but solemn. The ceremony included: (1) Presenting birthday incense and birthday candles, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Presidium takes their seats, (4) Play music, (5) Perform birthday salutations with three bows, (6) Shout slogans: "Long live the Republic of China" and "Long live Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek," (7) Play music, (8) Adjourn. At 6:00 PM, a banquet was held in the Eight Immortals Hall. During the banquet, Yu Qiaqing stood up and delivered a birthday speech, saying, "Today, leaders from all walks of life are here to celebrate Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday. Since Generalissimo Chiang led the Northern Expedition from Guangdong, ten years have passed in a flash. China's internal affairs have been settled from the difficult and arduous process, and the country has been stabilized. This year, domestic unification has been completed, and the provinces have had abundant harvests. The people of the whole country are excited. On the occasion of Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday, all sectors celebrate Generalissimo Chiang's birthday to show their enthusiasm and support. Generalissimo Chiang has worked hard and made great achievements. Generalissimo Chiang has not forgotten to serve the country and be filial to his parents. The country's difficulties are so severe, and Generalissimo Chiang has been able to persevere for ten years without diminishing his efforts. Today's birthday celebration is not for his own honor, but to dedicate all that is received to the country and the nation. The current public opinion is not the public opinion of the past. The current leader is not the leader of the past. I hope that the people of the whole country will be of one heart and one mind, follow Generalissimo Chiang, and complete the revolutionary cause." Huang Renzhi, Qian Xinzhi, and Du Yuesheng then delivered congratulatory speeches. The length of their words is omitted. The entertainment program included Ma Yunliang's "Adding Rank and Promotion," Li Wanchun's "God Presents Longevity," Zhao Ruquan and Zhou Xinfang's "Eight Hundred Eighty Years," Han Suqiu and Yun Yanxia's "Golden Jade Hole," Li Huisen, Li Huiliang, Li Huimin, and Li Huilan's "Little Nengren Temple," Shen Tiancui and Zhang Song's "Presenting the Map," Xiao Gaijiao Tian's "Siping Mountain," Zhao Peixin and Jin Suwen's "Playing Phoenix with Dragon," Li Wanchun's "Water Curtain Cave," Zhao Peixin, Li Wanchun, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Yuan Sen, and Sun Lanting's "Falling Horse Lake," and Ma Lianliang and Zhang Eyun's "Famen Temple." At 8:00 PM in the evening, fireworks were set off.

Railway Bureau Party and Workers Celebrate Birthday with Luncheon

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau, in celebration of Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday, had all stations along the two lines displaying flags and decorations. The various trains and locomotives in operation also displayed Party-State flags to mark the occasion. At 10:00 AM, they also joined the special Party Headquarters and labor union of the two lines to hold a birthday celebration ceremony in the auditorium on the seventh floor of the new building. Over 300 people attended, including staff members from various offices and committees from the Party Headquarters and union. Bureau Director Huang Boqiao presided over the ceremony, performing the rituals as required, and delivered a birthday speech, saying, "Generalissimo Chiang is the revolutionary leader of our Party and country. After decades of struggle, he has completed the great cause of unifying the country. His hardships and achievements are unsurpassed, and his merits will last forever. Today, we respectfully celebrate Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday to express the unanimous respect of the people." Standing Committee member Chen Chengshi of the Party Headquarters then reported, and they adjourned at 11:00 AM. During the meeting, a locomotive was dispatched to the North Station to sound its whistle for three minutes, and all on-duty staff members stood at attention to pay their respects. At 6:00 PM in the afternoon, a joint luncheon was held in the cafeteria on the seventh floor of the bureau building, with wonderful performances of Peking Opera singing and musical performances to add to the festivities.

Security Party Headquarters Enthusiastically Celebrates

Yesterday was Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. In addition to ordering its subordinate Party Headquarters at all levels to display flags to mark the occasion in their respective defense areas and to hold birthday celebration ceremonies, the Municipal Security Team Party Headquarters held its own birthday celebration ceremony. The meeting place was decorated simply and solemnly, with Party-State flags crossed at the entrance. Inside the hall, a portrait of Generalissimo Chiang was hung below the portrait of the Founding Father, with a banner above reading "Celebrating Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's Fiftieth Birthday." On both sides were couplets reading "Reviving and Assisting the Endangered, the People Depend on You; Establishing Benevolence and Upholding Righteousness, Boundless Longevity." Small Party-State flags and red and green paper flower decorations were hung all around. The ceremony began at 9:00 AM. After performing the rituals as required, Secretary-General Shi Shujiazhi of the Party Headquarters delivered a congratulatory speech, saying, "In celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, we should remember Generalissimo Chiang's spirit of saving the nation and the country, carry on his aspirations, strengthen national defense, and revive the nation. May Generalissimo Chiang's longevity be boundless, and may the nation and the country's longevity be boundless." The entire group then recited the Generalissimo's instructions to the military in unison, and finally shouted slogans. The atmosphere was enthusiastic and joyful, and their admiration for the leader was very sincere. The ceremony ended at 10:00 AM. The Party Headquarters colleagues held a dinner that evening.

Municipal Public Safety Bureau Celebrates Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Public Safety Bureau held a celebration ceremony for Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday at 8:00 AM yesterday morning in the Guangchang (plaza) in front of the Longhua Police Training Center. Several hundred people participated, including senior officers and student police officers, arranged in an orderly manner. After performing the rituals as required, Director Cai Jinjun gave a speech, first elaborating on the great significance of celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, and then recounting Generalissimo Chiang's history of sharing weal and woe with the late Founding Father, encouraging all staff and student police officers to uphold Generalissimo Chiang's spirit of fearlessness and take on the mission of eliminating the current domestic threats. He then recited "Military Personnel's Instructions." Finally, everyone shouted "Long live the Republic of China," "Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party," and "Long live Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek" in unison. The atmosphere among all the personnel was extremely enthusiastic. After the ceremony, the graduation ceremony for the thirty-second term of student police officers and the opening ceremony for the thirty-fourth term of student police officers were held. Director Cai gave an instructional speech, with many words of encouragement. Finally, awards were given to the graduating student police officers, and the award recipients expressed their gratitude as required.

City General Labor Union's Joyful Gathering

The City General Labor Union held a joyful birthday celebration gathering at its association building in Meijia Lane, Xiaonanmen, yesterday morning at 9:00 AM. Over 100 representatives from over 60 labor union organizations, including postal workers, Fourth District cigarette workers, and the Labor Association, attended, including Zhou Xuexiang, Shao Xubai, Zhao Shusheng, Zhang Kechang, Li Mengnan, Gong Yuting, Ye Xianggao, Long Peiyun, and Shui Xiangyun. Zhu Xuefan presided over the meeting, leading the birthday salutations, and delivered an opening speech, saying, "Celebrating Generalissimo Chiang's birthday: (1) the city's labor community should unite as one and support the leader; (2) strive for national economic construction and strengthen national defense; (3) unify the front and contribute our bodies and minds to the country, preserving the integrity of its territory and sovereignty." Standing Committee members Zhou Xuexiang and Li Mengnan then gave speeches in succession. The tea and snacks were served at 10:30 AM, and the meeting adjourned.

Seamen's Outing and Tower Climbing Competition

The Shanghai Seamen's Party Headquarters special commissioner Yang Hu, the Seamen's Union committee member Peng Bowei, secretary Wang Jiyi, Seamen's Branch committee members Lü Shuangxi, Cheng Yongming, and others, in celebration of Generalissimo Chiang's birthday, specially held a seamen's luncheon and joyful gathering yesterday at 12:00 PM in the party headquarters in Taili Lane, Zhaojiabang Road. In addition to Yang Hu, Peng Bowei, Lü Shuangxi, Cheng Yongming, and Wang Jiyi, over 100 people attended, including Li Jianbai, Wang Oumin, Mao Yufeng, and Lu Rongzhi. Citizens' Association Luncheon and Entertainment

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association's celebration of Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's birthday was quite enthusiastic. In addition to the district branches notifying citizens to display flags in celebration, all the association's executive and supervisory committee members and branch representatives also held a joyful gathering at the Bingshe Society in Cishuli, Yunnan Road, starting at 6:00 PM yesterday. First, they had a luncheon. During the luncheon, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Cao Zhigong, Liu Zhongying, Zhu Yangwu, and others gave speeches, explaining the significance of holding the joyful gathering and Generalissimo Chiang's revolutionary history in great detail. After the luncheon, a grand entertainment performance was held to add to the festivities. They dispersed in joy at midnight.

Christian Believers' Birthday Celebration Worship

The Shanghai Christian Association also held a prayer meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon at Moore Memorial Church on Yu Qiaqing Road to respectfully celebrate Chiang's birthday. Over 1,000 people attended, including Zhao Jinqing, Gao Fengchi, Cui Tongyue, Wang Wanbai, and Zhou Zhiyu. The presidium included Gao Fengchi, Cui Tongyue, and Zhu Guishen. The Bethel Choir sang hymns. Pastor Zhang Shaozeng preached a sermon. Zhao Jinqing, Zhu Guishen, and Chen Chunsheng prayed for the spiritual and physical well-being of Mr. and Mrs. Chiang, for domestic and foreign affairs, and for international peace. [They] asked for divine blessing. A photo was taken and tea and refreshments were served. It was also reported that the prayer meeting sent Generalissimo Chiang a large gold-edged leather-bound Bible as a birthday gift to mark the occasion.

Chinese Taoist Association's Celebration Ceremony

The Chinese Taoist Association had notified all temples to gather Taoist followers and piously perform repentance rituals for disaster relief and longevity on Generalissimo Chiang's birthday. Yesterday, all the temples conscientiously complied. It was said that the arrangements at Qingxu Temple and the Great King Temple were the most solemn and grand. On that day, the entrance of the Taoist Association was hung with colorful lanterns reading "Longevity for the Person, Longevity for the Country, Limitless and Boundless," and a plaque reading "Celebrating with the Country." At 9:00 AM, the association gathered members and faculty and students from the affiliated Hongdao Elementary School and held a celebration meeting. The chairman of the association and the school board led them to stand solemnly in the hall and pay their respects to the portrait of Generalissimo Chiang. They sang a celebration song together. Then, class teacher Wu Yunqian lectured on the significance of the celebration and Generalissimo Chiang's merits for the country and the people, and encouraged the students to practice the New Life Movement diligently and seek learning, create a great personality, serve with loyalty, and strive to save the country, taking Generalissimo Chiang as a model. After the lecture, the entire group shouted "Long live Generalissimo Chiang" three times, and then the meeting adjourned. A dinner was held in the evening.

Hebei Fellow-Townsmen Association Gathering and Celebration

All the staff members of the Hebei Fellow-Townsmen Association gathered at the association yesterday morning at 10:00 AM to respectfully celebrate Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday. The hall was decorated with colorful flowers, and the flowers were used to decorate the area around Generalissimo Chiang's portrait. Zhao Nangong also collected and wrote the four characters "Receiving Heaven's Mandate" from the Mao Gong Ding tripod and attached them below Generalissimo Chiang's portrait. The hall was simple, but extremely clean and solemn. At 11:00 AM, Secretary Director Fan Yumin called the assembly, and Standing Committee member Dong Shouquan led them to first bow to the portrait of the Founding Father, and then bow three times to the portrait of Generalissimo Chiang. Zhao Nangong reported on the brief history of Chiang's revolution, and said that Generalissimo Chiang has made a final decision on the current situation in Hebei and Chahar, and is actively preparing. Please trust Generalissimo Chiang, and he will not allow our Hebei and Chahar to become the result of the Northeast. After the ceremony, firecrackers were set off to express joy and celebration. It was also proposed to send a congratulatory telegram, which read, "To Chiang, President of the Administrative Yuan in Nanjing, O Sir, Hero of the Nation, your prestige and reputation shake and subdue the Rong. The great evolution is progressing, like the sun at its peak. The whole world celebrates together. O Sir, The Hebei Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai respectfully wishes you. [Seal]" At 12:30 PM, they had a luncheon, and dispersed in joy after 4:00 PM.

Grand Celebration by Various Sectors in the County

Yesterday was Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday. Over 50 representatives from various sectors in Shanghai County gathered at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall at 9:00 AM to open a celebration rally. The Minhang Guangci Hospital Boy Scout Band played music, and three other squads participated. After Chairman Jin Zuobin's report, County Magistrate Li Zhifu and County Party Headquarters Supervisory Committee Member Zhang Yi gave speeches, elaborating extensively on the commendable words and deeds of Generalissimo Chiang's life and his merits in governing the country and the military. Supervisory Committee Member Zhang further used the spirit of hard work, practical work, and tough work to encourage himself. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. Immediately afterward, the third district's citizen team was inspected at the County Public Sports Ground. The inspecting officials were County Magistrate Li Zhifu, Instructor Liu Shen, Education Bureau Director Zhu Changlin, District Chief Zhang Fengshan, and Commander-in-Chief Zhang Nanshan. 500 citizens participated, and their technical performance was proficient. [The inspection] stopped at 12:30 PM. Also, the County Party Headquarters sent a congratulatory telegram yesterday, which read, "To Vice Chairman Chiang of the Central Executive Committee, In recent years, the Party and the country have been plagued by many disasters and crises. You, sir, as the pillar of the stream, laid the foundation for the country on bedrock. Your plans and strategies rescued the people from the depths of despair. You hold the determination to resist foreign aggression and save the country, and set the grand plan of internal pacification and external resistance. You are diligent, brave, faithful, and loyal. Your virtuous and hardworking reputation is known to all. We are pleased to celebrate your fiftieth birthday. We send a telegram to express our sincere congratulations. We respectfully request your consideration. The Shanghai County Executive Committee of the Jiangsu Province branch of the Chinese Nationalist Party. [Seal]" Various sectors in Zhuanqiao held a celebration ceremony for Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek's fiftieth birthday at the Chongnong Hall yesterday morning (October 31st) at 6:00 AM. Over 2,000 people from various sectors, including the Party, government, agriculture, business, industry, academia, and the public, attended. Chongnong Hall could not accommodate everyone, so the venue was changed to Daidan Field. Zhang Yi was publicly elected as chairman. After the ceremony, the chairman reported, saying, "Since participating in the revolution, Generalissimo Chiang has only known the Party and the country, and has not known his own family. He followed the Founding Father to establish the Party army, led the Northern Expedition, unified the country, suppressed the Red bandits, strictly prohibited opium, promoted the New Life and National Economic Construction movements, and implemented citizen training. With the spirit of hard work, practical work, and tough work, and the courage to save the people, the country, and the world, his hard work and achievements are highly appreciated by the people. At this time of severe national crisis, we rely on the leader to lead the multitudes to save the country. From now on, we should take Generalissimo Chiang's will as our will and Generalissimo Chiang's spirit as our spirit. Under Generalissimo Chiang's guidance, we should work together with one heart and one mind to develop a new path for our Chinese nation. Now, on the occasion of Generalissimo Chiang's fiftieth birthday, all the agencies, groups, schools, and people in Zhuanqiao jointly celebrate to express our sincerity in loving and supporting the leader. However, the celebration is not limited to today. Now, our efforts are the way to repay Generalissimo Chiang." Each sector's representatives Ru Bocai, Zhang Nanshan, and Zhang Yun were asked to give speeches. The meeting adjourned with shouting slogans at 7:30 AM. After the meeting, Zhang Yi, on behalf of all sectors, sent a telegram to Generalissimo Chiang to express his congratulations. The telegram read, "To Chiang, President of the Administrative Yuan in Nanjing, Since you, sir, participated in the revolution, your achievements have been outstanding. You established the Party army, completed the Northern Expedition, unified the North and South, suppressed the Communist bandits, promoted the New Life and National Economic Construction movements, abolished miscellaneous taxes, and strictly prohibited opium. All those who are able to consolidate the national foundation and revive the nation, you, sir, lead the way. You are the savior of the people and the leader of the Party and the country. Now, on the occasion of your fiftieth birthday, we cherish your great virtues and are extremely grateful. In addition to jointly celebrating by various sectors, we send a special telegram to express our congratulations. We respectfully request your attention. Zhuanqiao representatives from various sectors in Shanghai County, Zhang Yi. [Seal]"

Maochang Employees Donate Salaries

The employees of the Huangpu Road Maochang Egg Factory have been extremely enthusiastic in donating to the government for the purchase of aircraft to present to Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek on his fiftieth birthday. The factory and the general manager personally had previously donated 1,000 yuan in national currency. Yesterday, all the employees, from the general manager to the workers, initiated a donation of one day's salary to the government, and collected a total of 632 yuan and nine cents in national currency, which has been sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for transfer to the Aviation Association. The factory distributed a notice in advance stating that anyone who did not agree could request to be exempted from donating, and there would be no coercion. As a result, no one requested to be exempted, showing that the desire to love and support the leader and strengthen national defense is the same for everyone. Even more remarkably, Mr. Carlton, an engineer and American refrigeration expert at the factory, and Mr. Pan Guoqi, the British deputy manager, were also very supportive, and each donated one day's salary, showing that this birthday celebration for Generalissimo Chiang is admired by both Chinese and foreigners.

Resolutions of the Henan Provincial Local Education Conference: Vigorously Implement National Defense Education and Rectify Schools at All Levels

(Kaifeng Express News) The Henan Provincial Local Education Administrative Conference opened on the morning of the 26th. The first general meeting and group review meetings were held in the afternoon. On the 27th, the second plenary session continued at 9:00 a.m., and the group review of funds and expenses was held at 2:00 p.m. At 4:00 p.m., the bureau chiefs visited Henan University. Proposals were discussed on the 28th in the morning and afternoon, and it was not until evening that the discussions were concluded. The originally scheduled closing ceremony was changed to the 29th. At 8:00 a.m. this morning, the bureau chiefs lined up to visit the Provincial Kaifeng Women's Normal School. The closing ceremony was held at 9:30 a.m., and in the afternoon, they visited the museum and other places. It is reported that after the meeting, they will all return to their counties. The resolutions of the past few days are recorded as follows: (1) Vigorously implement national defense education: resolution passed; (2) Establish a local education communication network to assist in guidance and research: resolution passed; (3) Stipulate measures for awarding outstanding teachers and staff in primary and secondary schools in various counties: resolution passed; (4) Stipulate the standards for the appointment of education committee members in school districts in various counties and improve their treatment: resolution passed; (5) Stipulate that teachers and staff in primary and secondary schools in various counties should be trained separately in a centralized manner: resolution passed; (6) Regularly rotate and observe county school inspectors in various counties: resolution passed; (7) Stipulate the outline for local education supervision: resolution passed; (8) Education authorities in various counties should prepare budgets and accounts, and implement them earnestly to achieve balanced development: resolution passed; (10) Improve the secondary education programs in various counties: resolution passed; the text was handed over to the secretariat of the general assembly for revision; (11) Reorganize the rural primary schools in various counties; (12) Reorganize the complete primary schools in various counties; (13) How to improve the treatment of primary school teachers: please submit to the public for decision; resolutions for the above three proposals: approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (14) Rectify social education in various counties; (15) Train local social education talents: resolutions for the above two proposals: approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (16) Maintain the independence of education funding in various counties: resolution passed with amendments; (17) Raise additional education funds for various counties: resolution passed; (18) All surcharges on deed taxes in various counties, in addition to the general surcharges, should be allocated to education funds: resolution passed to request the Department of Education to handle them separately based on the circumstances of each county; (19) Request that a certain amount of the collected and stored joint guarantee and education funds be allocated to education to comply with the original proposal: resolution approved in principle and requested the Department of Education to select and implement it; (20) Propose maintaining the original number of apportioned taxes to maintain education funds: resolution passed with amendments; (21) Determine the funding for district, township, and town primary schools to facilitate the development of education: resolution approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (22) Determine the management methods for township education funds: resolution passed; (23) Subsidies for offsetting exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies should be allocated monthly according to the amount to maintain education funds: resolution passed; (24) Education funds in various counties should be spent in accordance with the expenditure standards of the Education Bureau, and the Department of Finance should not reduce or change the standards; (25) Amend the current expenditure standards for Education Bureau funds; (26) If the budgeted funds for the Education Bureau in various counties are insufficient, it is proposed to increase them appropriately and allow Bureaus of the 2nd, 4th and 5th levels to add a clerk; (27) The wages of Education Bureau staff should be divided into grades and included in the expenditure standards for education funds: resolutions for the above four proposals: combined and sent to the Department for consideration; (28) Stipulate the standards for inspection travel expenses: resolution approved in principle, and the methods were sent to the Department of Education for reference; (29) The expenses required for setting up free and public-funded quotas in county-level schools at all levels should be allocated from county local funds to facilitate implementation: resolution passed; (30) From which item of funding should the travel and accommodation expenses of trainees in various counties be paid? Please have the relevant authorities clearly stipulate this for compliance: resolution passed; (31) It is proposed that the provincial government separately issue letters to national and provincial secondary schools and above, prohibiting them from sending letters to county government education bureaus requesting the allocation of subsidies or travel expenses for visits: resolution passed; (32) Determine the funding for rural primary schools: resolution approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (33) Request the allocation of provincial funds to subsidize secondary schools: resolution passed; (34) Implement vocational-education cooperation to develop vocational education in various counties: resolution passed; (35) Centralize the scientific equipment of county-level schools at all levels to improve teaching efficiency: resolution for the Department of Education to consider; (36) Increase social education funding in accordance with the standards set by the Ministry to promote the development of social education in various counties: resolution passed; (37) Education patrol teams should be established in various counties: resolution approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (38) The people's education in various counties is proposed to be abolished uniformly, and the funds are transferred to promote people's education: resolution approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for selection and implementation; (39) Each county and district should establish a central people's school, with members of the local militia training teams as students: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; (40) Control operas and instill national sentiments: resolution sent to the Department of Education for overall planning; (41) Determine methods for in-service training of primary school teachers to increase educational efficiency: resolution passed; (42) Formulate specific methods for funding compulsory education in various counties: resolution passed; (43) Propose changing the current short-term compulsory education system to facilitate its implementation: resolution approved in principle and submitted to the Department of Education for referral to the Ministry of Education for approval; (44) Propose ordering county training institutes to train short-term primary school teachers to improve their skills: resolution passed; (45) Supplement and compile textbooks for compulsory short-term primary schools to facilitate compliance: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; (46) Request strict measures to ban private schools to facilitate rural education: resolution passed; (47) Stipulate that joint guarantees should be established for primary schools in various counties: resolution approved in principle and sent to the Department of Education for reference; (48) Abolish missionary schools: resolution passed; (49) Reduce the ranking of the Education Bureau and increase operating expenses: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; (50) Organize district education inspection teams: resolution passed; (51) Increase the efficiency of local education administration throughout the province: resolution passed; (52) Organize local education administrative personnel to form visiting groups: resolution approved in principle and sent to the Department of Education for reference; (53) Popularize local education and collect and distribute funding methods: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; Temporary motions: (1) This month, the 31st is Chairman Chiang's 50th birthday. It is proposed to send a congratulatory telegram in the name of the conference: resolution: unanimously passed by the entire assembly, and the telegram was handed over to the secretariat of the conference for drafting and dispatch; (2) Over the years, the officers and soldiers who have suppressed bandits have made outstanding contributions to clearing out the remnants of bandits and recovering bandit areas. It is proposed to send a message of appreciation in the name of the conference: resolution unanimously passed by the entire assembly, and the telegram was handed over to the secretariat of the conference for drafting and dispatch; (3) Experimental classes of two-and-a-half-year systems should be established in various counties in the province: resolution passed; (4) Propose that the Wanzhou County Ceramic Vocational School be reorganized: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; (5) Propose that the Department of Education establish mining and sericulture schools to adhere to the principle of running schools according to local conditions and establishing education according to needs: resolution sent to the Department of Education for reference; (6) Secondary schools and teachers in various counties must join the Aviation Construction Association as members: resolution passed. (Dispatch from the 29th)

Boy Scouts of China General Association: Second Anniversary of Establishment

The Boy Scouts of this city hold celebrations

The Boy Scouts of China General Association has been established since November 1, 1934, and it has been two years. The Municipal Boy Scout Council received a telegram from the General Association yesterday, saying, "It is hereby notified that November 1st this year is the first anniversary of the establishment of the Association. Celebrations should be held to commemorate it. Celebration methods have been formulated and are hereby promulgated by telegram. Boy Scouts in various provinces, cities, and counties will hold celebration ceremonies in their respective locations at 1:00 p.m. on that day." It is reported that the Municipal Boy Scout Council has instructed various troops to convene all Boy Scouts in their respective troops at 1:00 p.m. today to hold celebration ceremonies to mark the anniversary.

Hard Court Tennis Tournament Begins Yesterday: Wang Shuzi Loses to Korasa, Yan Jingmei Eliminated in Group Stage

The 24th French Concession General Association Autumn Hard Court Tennis Championship kicked off yesterday. All twelve matches on the first day were men's and women's singles. Among the Chinese players in the men's singles, six attended yesterday. Except for Chen Yi and Sun Qifang, who repeatedly withdrew indoors to practice, only one had to be eliminated. The rest were only Zhu Shuzi, who lost to Korasa, Li Pijiu, Li Guofan, Sun Qifang, and Zhou Guanjun. In addition, the group results, except for Zhou Guanjun's victory over Dickson, which was slightly close in the first set, the rest became one-sided. The most regrettable thing is that Miss Yan Jingjiang, the only Chinese player in the women's competition, unfortunately lost miserably to Miss Mato, so the future battle for dominance will all be blue-eyed. As for the men's singles, because Carson left Japan and Bao Huadefu gave up, the prediction for the championship should be a battle between Li Pizu, a strong player from Beijing, and Korasa, a Portuguese general from the French Concession. Except for Zhou Shesuan, who unexpectedly defeated Ke in the second and third weeks, Li Pizu will meet Shi Yayu in the semi-finals, and Li Ke's entry into the final week will also be an undisputed fact. Tennis Friendly Match: China Wins Tongji

——Six to One——

The China Tennis Club agreed to a friendly match yesterday with the Tongji team, the champion of this year's university tennis tournament. There were four singles and three doubles matches. The players from both sides were focused and determined to learn from each other. As a result, the China Club won 6 to 1 thanks to its balanced talent, cooperative effort, and the help of Taiwan Cup player Cai Huiquan. It is reported that Cai Fang returned to Shanghai from Europe at the end of last week and will be staying in Shanghai for a long time. He plans to organize a tennis club to improve the level of tennis in the city and is currently actively planning it. The scores are recorded below:

Pudong YMCA: Plans to Build a Community Fitness Room

The Shanghai YMCA Pudong Branch spares no effort in various social services. It is reported that a joint meeting was held yesterday. The general secretary, Mr. Lu Ganchen, the general secretary, Mr. Luo Weilian, the directors of various departments, and all the staff of the branch were present. In addition to reporting on past work, the future direction was also discussed. The case that Pudong lacks a perfect and large fitness room was of the greatest concern. It was decided that a fitness room would be built in the near future to improve public health. At the same time, a larger branch office will be built to facilitate the promotion of social welfare undertakings. The staff of the branch have been appointed to actively study the various implementation plans so that construction can begin soon.

Skotto Cup Preliminary Round: French Business Eliminates Schalke

5 to 2, First Half 2 to 1

Western Union Football, French Business met Schalke yesterday in the Skotto League preliminaries. Although French Business played with a well-organized team, they were casual because their opponents were mediocre. As a result, Schalke opened the scoring first in the seventh minute. Local News

Industry and Commerce Passed the Tenth Day Yesterday: Lively Market, Reduced Interbank Lending, and Money Shops Have Repaid Their Loans One After Another

Yesterday was the tenth day period for Shanghai industry and commerce. All industries passed it safely due to sufficient preparation. Although the Central, China, and Communications Banks continued to handle interbank lending as usual, the lending was reduced due to the lively market, and the money shops have repaid their loans one after another. The details are recorded below.

Easy Credit

The Central, China, and Communications Banks, in order to regulate interbank finance, jointly organized a lending committee to handle lending matters for various banks and shops. All banks and shops can apply to the committee for lending with deeds, goods, and bonds as collateral. This year's tenth day was very lively because of the bumper harvest of agricultural products and increased purchasing power. Therefore, the credit in Shanghai was easy, and the applications for lending from the Central, China, and Communications Banks from various banks and shops decreased. For example, the foreign exchange rate in the money market was still 8% in both the morning and afternoon sessions yesterday, which shows that credit was easy.

Safely Passed the Tenth Day

All industries had made considerable preparations for this year's tenth day. At the same time, the Shanghai-Ningbo money shops provided accommodation for long-term credit loans that were due, so there was no emergency situation in the market yesterday, which was very different from the tenth days in previous years. The interest rate for new long-term credit loans made by various money shops is only between 8 and 10 yuan for those with good credit. The procedures for extending the term to the fourth day of next year have been fully completed, and all industries have safely passed the difficult hurdle of the tenth day.

Loans Repaid

Of the 18 million yuan that various money shops borrowed from the lending committee of the Central, China, and Communications Banks during the Dragon Boat Festival last year, after the borrowing money shops repaid in succession, only the loans borrowed by the Henglai and Hengxing shops, which are responsible for collecting accounts, have not been repaid. Now the two shops have taken measures to collect the loans they have made in order to repay the loans to the banks. However, these loans all have reliable collateral, so the three banks have repeatedly allowed the two shops to extend the repayment period. Because it is regulating interbank finance, the interest rate is 8% per annum.

Suma Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday: Discusses Japan's Diplomatic Policy

Central News Agency reports that Suma, First Secretary of the Japanese Embassy in China and Consul General in Beijing, returned to Japan on October 22 under the order of Ambassador Kawagoe to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on Ambassador Kawagoe's negotiations with Foreign Minister Zhang on adjusting Sino-Japanese issues and to request instructions on future policies. He has completed his work and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 9:30 on the French mail ship Aramis. Takahashi, the representative of the Japanese delegation, welcomed him at the port. After disembarking, he went to the Japanese Consulate to rest. Then he met with Japanese diplomatic officials in Shanghai. He took the express train to Beijing at 1:25 p.m. to visit Ambassador Kawagoe and report back. A reporter from the Central News Agency met Suma on the ship. According to the interview,

No Concessions in Negotiations with China

According to Suma, I returned to Japan under the order of Ambassador Kawagoe to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and to request instructions. Because of the short time, I only stayed in Tokyo for two days. Japan's diplomatic policy toward China, whether in the government or among the people, still adheres to the original position and will not make concessions. Therefore, I did not bring the so-called new instructions this time.

Answers to Reporters' Questions: Says There is a Way

Suma continued, it is difficult to predict whether the Sino-Japanese negotiations can be resolved peacefully. However, according to my observation, the Sino-Japanese negotiations will not break down, and there is a way to resolve them peacefully. When the reporter asked how it could not break down if Japan's diplomatic policy toward China still adhered to the original position and would not make concessions, Suma smiled and replied that there was a way to not break down. As for Japan's views on the so-called "special status of North China" and "joint anti-communism," Suma did not make a clear statement.

No Statement on Credit Loans

Suma also did not make a clear statement on the Tokyo telegram that the Japanese government and people, in order to promote trade with China, would use the United Kingdom as a model and provide short-term credit loans to China. He only indicated that he had not heard of it when he was in Tokyo.

Arrived in Beijing in the Afternoon to Visit Kawagoe

After Suma disembarked, he returned to the consulate to rest. Then he met with Navy Attaché Sato, Councilor Wakasugi, and Intelligence Minister Yoshioka of the embassy. At 1:25 p.m., he left Shanghai with Secretary Wakasugi, Yoshioka, and Sone on the express train to Beijing to visit Ambassador Kawagoe and report back. The date of the seventh meeting between Kawagoe and our Foreign Minister Zhang will be determined after Suma arrives in Beijing.

Hong Kong-Shanghai Route to Open on the 5th of this Month; Simultaneous Commencement of Service Between China and the UK Marks a New Era for Aviation in the Far East; Full Sino-US Air Service Also Imminent

The China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) officially announced yesterday that the Hong Kong station is scheduled to open on November 5th. On the same day, direct air service will commence, formally connecting with British Overseas Airways Corporation (BOAC). Full Sino-US air service is also expected to officially launch within this month. A detailed report from a Shenzhou News Agency reporter is as follows:

Hong Kong Station to Open on the 5th of This Month

Yesterday, a CNAC representative officially announced that the establishment of a CNAC station in Hong Kong has been successfully negotiated between China and the UK. The British government's operating license has been obtained by CNAC. Preparations for the station's facilities are actively underway. The official opening date is set for November 5th. The flight will depart from Shanghai at 6:30 AM and arrive in Hong Kong at 2:45 PM the same day. The northbound flight is scheduled to depart from Hong Kong at 7:30 AM on the 6th and arrive in Shanghai at 3:45 PM the same day. Initially, there will be three round-trip flights per week. Current bookings for the inaugural Hong Kong-Shanghai flights are extremely enthusiastic. Flight frequency will be increased as needed to meet demand. The one-way ticket price between Shanghai and Hong Kong is 200 yuan, and a round-trip ticket is 390 yuan.

Simultaneous Commencement of Service Between China and the UK

The China National Aviation Corporation is handling the Hong Kong station opening on the Chinese side, while British Overseas Airways Corporation is handling it on the British side. Therefore, after the Hong Kong station opens on the 5th, the CNAC Shanghai-Guangdong route and the BOAC Far East route will also officially connect on the same day. From then on, passengers and mail between China and the UK can reach London via the joint CNAC-BOAC route. The spatial transportation between these two major Eastern and Western nations can thus be mutually connected, greatly facilitating travel and marking a new era for aviation in the Far East.

Full Sino-US Air Service Also to Be Established

With the CNAC Hong Kong station established, full Sino-US air service will also commence in the shortest possible time. Both Mr. Qu Libo, General Manager of Pan American Airways, and Mr. Witner, Chairman of the Board, have completed a test flight of the full Sino-US route and are currently conducting inspections in China. The date of the full Sino-US air service launch will be announced after Mr. Qu and Mr. Witner return to the United States and make a decision. Mr. Qu has already transited through London on his way back to the United States from Hong Kong. Mr. and Mrs. Witner and American media mogul Mr. Howard also took a CNAC flight from Shanghai to Guangzhou and then Hong Kong yesterday morning to catch a ship to Manila and then a Sino-US flight back to the United States. Once the Sino-US route is launched in the very near future, the three major trunk routes in the Far East—China-UK, China-France, and China-US—will all be completed.

New Aircraft to Be Deployed to China to Meet Demand

After the CNAC Shanghai-Guangdong route and Hong Kong station open, passenger and mail traffic are expected to be very heavy. Therefore, the company has already ordered two large Sikorsky flying boats from the United States, each capable of carrying approximately sixteen passengers. The internal equipment is also extremely complete. They are expected to arrive in China around the end of this year and will then be deployed on the Shanghai-Guangdong route and flight frequency will be increased. In addition, DC-3 Douglas jumbo landplanes will also continue to be delivered to China for deployment.

Execution of Li Guojie Case; Order to Provide Assets Within Half a Month; Li Has Petitioned the Executive Yuan for Exemption; Plaintiff Requests Bankruptcy Proceedings

Li Guojie, the former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (CMSNC), mortgaged four warehouses to the China General Edison Company without authorization and entered into a charter agreement with the Dalae Steamship Company, thereby harming national sovereignty. In order to establish the contract, Li bribed Chen Fumu, the director of the CMSNC, with a commission of 700,000 taels of silver. Zhu Jiajhua, the former Minister of Transportation, investigated and prosecuted the case. The Supreme Court ultimately sentenced Li Guojie to eight months of imprisonment with a two-year suspended sentence. He was also ordered to return the 700,000 taels of silver to CMSNC for the damages and interest accrued from the date of the damage, amounting to a total of 1.2 million taels. Li Sihao, the current chairman of the Economic Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, and Mr. Yu Qiaqing, a business leader in this city, posted bail on June 6th of this year for the civil lawsuit portion of the case. However, almost five months have passed since the bail was posted without a single payment. CMSNC has also published rewards to locate Li Guojie's private property, but without success. CMSNC filed a petition with the local court to continue the execution. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Judge Yu Lude convened an execution hearing. Jiang Hechun, an attorney representing CMSNC, and Lu Shifang and Wu Taiyu, attorneys representing Li Guojie as assistants, reported to the court. Attorney Jiang, representing the plaintiff, stated that the execution of the civil lawsuit was attached to the criminal case. Since June 6th, when bail was posted, and in July, when notice was served for the reporting of assets, the defendant was ordered to pay at least one-tenth of the amount, but has not paid a single cent to date. Therefore, he requested the court to pursue the principal amount of 700,000 taels of silver and the interest. At this point, the judge asked Li Guojie, "You should not delay payment." Li replied, "I should abide by the court's judgment, but I have no assets, so I am trying my best to find a solution." The judge asked, "Then how will you handle it?" Li replied, "CMSNC has already offered a reward to find my property." At this point, his attorney, Lu, stated, "CMSNC belongs to the Ministry of Transportation, and the Ministry of Transportation belongs to the Executive Yuan. Li Guojie was implicated due to official duties, so he has submitted a petition to the Premier of the Executive Yuan for exemption from payment." The judge said, "This case is now a legal issue. Regarding the debt, it cannot be suspended unless the creditor applies to dismiss the case. Your request today is without legal basis." Attorney Jiang, representing the plaintiff, stated, "The defendant was previously detained for three years and did not settle the debt. The reward offered to find his assets has only uncovered two properties that are currently under investigation. If we drag this on for another year or six months and still have no results, what can we do? Therefore, the plaintiff requests either an order for detention or a request for bankruptcy proceedings under the court's authority." Attorney Lu, representing the defendant, stated, "The defendant is a person of standing and does not wish to declare bankruptcy." Thereupon, Attorney Jiang, representing the plaintiff, requested that the case be handled according to bankruptcy law, while the defendant's attorney objected. After arguing, the judge ordered the defendant to provide assets within half a month and adjourned the court.

Shanghai Rainfall Seven Inches Less Than Last Year; Rainfall in the Yangtze River Basin Even Scarcer

Since the beginning of autumn, Shanghai has experienced scarce rainfall, leading to a gradual drought. Farmers in the suburbs are eagerly awaiting rain. At the same time, the water level of the Yangtze River is steadily drying up, making navigation increasingly difficult. The situation is summarized below:

This Year's Rainfall

According to a reporter from the Datong News Agency who inquired with the Hydrology Department of the Xunpu General Bureau, the rainfall record for Shanghai from January 1st to October 31st of this year is only 33.68 inches. Compared to the same period last year (also January to the end of October), which had 40.75 inches, the rainfall this year has decreased by more than 7.07 inches.

Two-Month Comparison

Comparing September and October, Shanghai's rainfall in September of last year was 4.8 inches, while it was only 1.7 inches in September of this year. Last year's rainfall in October was 1.72 inches, while there was absolutely no rainfall in October of this year. This type of autumn drought is rare in recent years. No wonder farmers in the suburbs are eagerly awaiting rain. It is also understood that rainfall in the Yangtze River basin this year is even less than in Shanghai, so it is only natural that the river water is drying up.

Yesterday Morning's Heavy Fog

Shanghai has seen hazy conditions for several consecutive nights, with the fog being especially heavy yesterday morning. It was difficult to recognize faces even at close range. The Huangpu River was misty, as if locked in by a heavy fog. As a result, all sails temporarily ceased rowing, and many ocean-going vessels remained outside the port. The heavy fog only dissipated around 9:00 AM, after which water traffic resumed. The CNAC Shanghai-Hankou flight was also delayed yesterday morning.

Bao Gang, a lawyer, was sued in the local court by Cui Changgui, a driver for the Special Task Force of the Shanghai Municipal Police, for seducing his fiancée, Yang Yuehua, and instigating a divorce, hiding her in Chuansha. He stopped him and accompanied him to the Wu Gong Hotel in the International Settlement, ostensibly to discuss the matter, and kept watch overnight. The guarantor, Huang Zhichang, testified about Bao Gang's conduct and stated that he was now unwilling to act as guarantor and requested to withdraw the guaranty. At this point, Bao Gang said, "I really had no intention of fleeing. They misunderstood." He requested to provide another guaranty. The judge said, "You are a lawyer and should know the law. You should abide by the law. Your current foolish behavior is really detrimental to you. Your request for guaranty is now denied. We will wait until after the judgment." National Products Production and Sales Association Invites Physician from Health Association to Lecture; Factory Leaders Express Deep Agreement

The Shanghai Health Assurance Association has recently seen its work develop rapidly, with the total number of participating groups and individual members reaching more than 7,000. An average of about 50 people come to the association for diagnosis every day. The physicians of various specialties provide careful diagnosis and treatment, almost bringing back life, deeply winning the trust of members. Various national products factories in this city have aroused common attention to this public welfare cause of health protection. In order to understand the purpose and content of the association, they have successively invited the association to give public lectures. The association, based on its responsibilities, is extremely willing to closely contact the industrial and commercial circles in order to protect the health of laborers and reduce the pain of diseases. Yesterday noon, the China National Products Production and Sales Association held a luncheon at Zhengyi Society. More than 100 factory leaders attended. Mr. Wang Zhixin presided over the meeting. After delivering an introductory speech, Mr. Chen Zhongjiu, the executive director of the Health Association, delivered a speech, saying that in recent years, major factories have been able to pay attention to labor hygiene and medical affairs in response to the needs of the times. Each factory employs a factory doctor specifically for the treatment of employees. However, with the progress of modern medicine, one or two factory doctors can hardly treat various diseases. It is necessary to have specialized medical consultations. The establishment of the Health Association meets the needs of this kind of fact. The association employs specialized doctors of various departments. Once a factory joins as a member, it can obtain the consultation of specialized doctors of various departments at a comparable price, which is the most economical and appropriate method. Subsequently, Dr. Li Zhongyong, the director of the association, delivered a speech, saying that the industrial sector requires an increase in production and work efficiency. It is necessary to first pay attention to the soundness of the workers' bodies. The Municipal Health Association is willing to dedicate its greatest efforts to this. First, it stipulates group membership to reduce membership fees; second, it provides specialized treatment to obtain expert consultation; and third, it guides factory hygiene and prevents the spread of diseases. The representatives expressed deep agreement with the opinions of Mr. Chen and Dr. Li. The meeting ended at half past two.

Jiang Erbao Pregnant; Abortion Death Requires Autopsy; Ju Jiuhua Arrested for Causing the Incident; Involved Zhou Wang and Chen
